# Welcome to [Wikipedia](/wiki/Wikipedia "Wikipedia")

,
the [free](/wiki/Free_content "Free content") [encyclopedia](/wiki/Encyclopedia "Encyclopedia") that [anyone can edit](/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_Wikipedia "Help:Introduction to Wikipedia").

## From today's featured article

The [Hearst Tower](/wiki/Hearst_Tower_(Manhattan) "Hearst Tower (Manhattan)") is a building at the southwest corner of [57th Street](/wiki/57th_Street_(Manhattan) "57th Street (Manhattan)") and [Eighth Avenue](/wiki/Eighth_Avenue_(Manhattan) "Eighth Avenue (Manhattan)"), near [Columbus Circle](/wiki/Columbus_Circle "Columbus Circle"), in the [Midtown Manhattan](/wiki/Midtown_Manhattan "Midtown Manhattan") neighborhood of [New York City](/wiki/New_York_City "New York City"), U.S. It is the world headquarters of the media conglomerate [Hearst Communications](/wiki/Hearst_Communications "Hearst Communications"), housing many of the firm's publications and communications companies. The Hearst Tower consists of two sections, with a total height of 597 feet (182Â m) and 46 stories. The six lowest stories form the original Hearst Magazine Building (also known as the International Magazine Building), designed by [Joseph Urban](/wiki/Joseph_Urban "Joseph Urban") and [George B. Post & Sons](/wiki/George_B._Post "George B. Post"), and completed in 1928. Above it is the Hearst Tower addition, designed by [Norman Foster](/wiki/Norman_Foster "Norman Foster") and finished in 2006. The original structure is clad with stone and contains six [pylons](/wiki/Pylon_(architecture)#Revival_architecture "Pylon (architecture)") with sculptural groups. The tower section has a glass-and-metal [faÃ§ade](/wiki/Fa%C3%A7ade "FaÃ§ade") arranged as a [diagrid](/wiki/Diagrid "Diagrid"), or diagonal grid, which doubles as its structural system. ([FullÂ article...](/wiki/Hearst_Tower_(Manhattan) "Hearst Tower (Manhattan)"))

## On this day

[December 29](/wiki/December_29 "December 29")

Terminal at LaGuardia Airport after the 1975 bombing

- [1845](/wiki/1845 "1845") â€“ The [Republic of Texas](/wiki/Republic_of_Texas "Republic of Texas") [was annexed](/wiki/Texas_annexation "Texas annexation") by the United States, becoming [the 28th state](/wiki/Texas "Texas") to be [admitted to the Union](/wiki/Admission_to_the_Union "Admission to the Union").
- [1860](/wiki/1860 "1860") â€“ To counter the [French Navy](/wiki/French_Navy "French Navy")'s [Gloire](/wiki/French_ironclad_Gloire "French ironclad Gloire"), the world's first [ironclad warship](/wiki/Ironclad_warship "Ironclad warship"), the [Royal Navy](/wiki/Royal_Navy "Royal Navy") launched [HMSÂ Warrior](/wiki/HMS_Warrior_(1860) "HMS Warrior (1860)"), the world's first iron-hulled armoured warship.
- [1890](/wiki/1890 "1890") â€“ [Sioux Wars](/wiki/Sioux_Wars "Sioux Wars"): The [United States Army](/wiki/United_States_Army "United States Army") killed 250 to 300 [Lakota](/wiki/Lakota_people "Lakota people") men, women and children at the [Wounded Knee Massacre](/wiki/Wounded_Knee_Massacre "Wounded Knee Massacre"), beginning the [Ghost Dance War](/wiki/Ghost_Dance_War "Ghost Dance War").
- [1915](/wiki/1915 "1915") â€“ [First World War](/wiki/World_War_I "World War I"): The French parliament [passed a law](/wiki/French_law_of_29_December_1915 "French law of 29 December 1915") granting the land occupied by British war graves as "the free gift of the French people".
- [1975](/wiki/1975 "1975") â€“ Planted by unknown perpetrators, [a bomb exploded](/wiki/1975_LaGuardia_Airport_bombing "1975 LaGuardia Airport bombing") (aftermath pictured) at [LaGuardia Airport](/wiki/LaGuardia_Airport "LaGuardia Airport") in New York City, killing 11 people and seriously injuring 74 others.

## From today's featured list

Jimi Hendrix

American musician [Jimi Hendrix](/wiki/Jimi_Hendrix "Jimi Hendrix") [recorded more than 170 songs during his career from 1966 to 1970](/wiki/List_of_songs_recorded_by_Jimi_Hendrix "List of songs recorded by Jimi Hendrix"). Often considered one of the most accomplished and influential electric guitarists, Hendrix wrote most of his own material in a variety of styles. Some show his [blues](/wiki/Blues "Blues") and [R&B](/wiki/Rhythm_and_blues "Rhythm and blues") roots, and others incorporate [jazz](/wiki/Jazz "Jazz") and early [funk](/wiki/Funk "Funk") influences. Some songs, such as "[Purple Haze](/wiki/Purple_Haze "Purple Haze")", "[Voodoo Child (Slight Return)](/wiki/Voodoo_Child_(Slight_Return) "Voodoo Child (Slight Return)")", and "[Machine Gun](/wiki/Machine_Gun_(Jimi_Hendrix_song) "Machine Gun (Jimi Hendrix song)")", feature his guitar-dominated [hard rock](/wiki/Hard_rock "Hard rock") and [psychedelic rock](/wiki/Psychedelic_rock "Psychedelic rock") sound, while others including "[The Wind Cries Mary](/wiki/The_Wind_Cries_Mary "The Wind Cries Mary")" and "[Little Wing](/wiki/Little_Wing "Little Wing")" take a slower, more melodic approach. Two of his best-known single releases were written by others: "[Hey Joe](/wiki/Hey_Joe "Hey Joe")" by [Billy Roberts](/wiki/Billy_Roberts "Billy Roberts") and "[All Along the Watchtower](/wiki/All_Along_the_Watchtower "All Along the Watchtower")" by [Bob Dylan](/wiki/Bob_Dylan "Bob Dylan"). Hendrix supplied his own interpretations, however, which gave them a much different character than the originals. ([FullÂ list...](/wiki/List_of_songs_recorded_by_Jimi_Hendrix "List of songs recorded by Jimi Hendrix"))

## Today's featured picture

The [red-tailed laughingthrush](/wiki/Red-tailed_laughingthrush "Red-tailed laughingthrush") (Trochalopteron milnei) is a species of bird in the family Leiothrichidae, the [laughingthrushes](/wiki/Laughingthrush "Laughingthrush"). It is found in the montane forests of Myanmar, Laos, southern China, and central Vietnam. These birds mainly inhabit the understorey of broadleaf evergreen forests, usually living at an elevation of 1,800 to 2,500 metres (5,900 to 8,200Â ft) above sea level. The red-tailed laughingthrush has an overall length of about 26 to 28 centimetres (10 to 11Â in) and a weight of about 66 to 93 grams (2.3 to 3.3Â oz). It is dull ochrous-grey, with a bright rufous-chestnut crown and a blackish face, with whitish ear-coverts. The wings and tail are crimson, and the sexes are similar in appearance. The species feeds mainly on insects and small arthropods, but sometimes also takes berries and fruits. Its breeding season lasts from April to June, and it makes nests composed principally of grasses and bamboo leaves. This red-tailed laughingthrush was photographed in a nature reserve near [Ngá»c Linh](/wiki/Ng%E1%BB%8Dc_Linh "Ngá»c Linh"), a mountain in central Vietnam.

Photograph credit: [JJÂ Harrison](/wiki/User:JJ_Harrison "User:JJ Harrison")

[Complete list of Wikimedia projects](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Complete_list_of_Wikimedia_projects "Special:MyLanguage/Complete list of Wikimedia projects") â€” [List of Wikimedia projects by size](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/List_of_Wikimedia_projects_by_size "Special:MyLanguage/List of Wikimedia projects by size")

This page contains information about all 358 languages for which official [Wikipedias](/wiki/Wikipedia "Wikipedia") have been created under the auspices of the [Wikimedia Foundation](/wiki/Wikimedia_Foundation "Wikimedia Foundation"). The table below, however, excludes [16 Wikipedias that were closed](#Closed_and_read-only) and 11 of them were moved to the [Wikimedia Incubator](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/ "incubator:") for further development, leaving a current total of 342 active Wikipedias. Content in other languages is being developed at the Wikimedia Incubator; languages which meet [certain criteria](/wiki/Language_proposal_policy "Language proposal policy") can get their own [wikis](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/wiki "w:wiki").

The table entries are ordered by current article count. Each entry gives the language name in English (linked to the English Wikipedia article for the language); its "local name" (i.e. in the language itself); the [language code](/wiki/Special:SiteMatrix "Special:SiteMatrix") used in the wiki's [URL](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/URL "w:URL") address and in [interwiki links](/wiki/Help:Interwiki_linking "Help:Interwiki linking") to it (linked to the local Main Page); and statistics on articles, edits, administrators, users, active users, and images (each linked to an appropriate local special page).

To start a Wikipedia in a new language, please see our [language proposal policy](/wiki/Language_proposal_policy "Language proposal policy") and [the Incubator manual](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Help:Manual "incubator:Help:Manual"). Note: Just adding a link here does not create a new Wikipedia, nor does it serve to request that one be created.

If a wiki becomes active and is not listed here, please post a notice on [this article's talk page](/wiki/Talk:List_of_Wikipedias "Talk:List of Wikipedias"), including a link to all the relevant Wikipedia pages, and help promote the effort by announcing it on the [Wikipedia-L](/wiki/Mailing_lists/Overview#Project_mailing_lists "Mailing lists/Overview") mailing list, and at [Wikimedia News](/wiki/Wikimedia_News "Wikimedia News").

The tables here are maintained automatically based on statistics collected by a bot four times a day, so it is not necessary to "manually" update the table. (The way this is being done makes that impossible, anyway.) If something is wrong with an entry other than simply having slightly outdated statistics, post about it on the [talk page](/wiki/Talk:List_of_Wikipedias "Talk:List of Wikipedias").

- [List of Wikipedias by edits per article](/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_edits_per_article "List of Wikipedias by edits per article") and [depth](/wiki/Wikipedia_article_depth "Wikipedia article depth") (both updated every 6 hours)
- [List of Wikipedias by language group](/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_language_group "List of Wikipedias by language group") and [family](/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_language_family "List of Wikipedias by language family") (both updated every 6 hours) and [language families as a tree](/wiki/Tree_of_Wikimedia_wikis_by_language_family "Tree of Wikimedia wikis by language family") (not just Wikipedias)
- [List of Wikipedias by country](/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_country "List of Wikipedias by country") (updated manually)
- [List of Wikipedias by speakers per article](/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_speakers_per_article "List of Wikipedias by speakers per article") (updated every 6 hours)
- [List of Wikipedias by sample of articles](/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_sample_of_articles "List of Wikipedias by sample of articles") and [expanded sample of articles](/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_by_expanded_sample_of_articles "List of Wikipedias by expanded sample of articles") (both updated monthly)
- [List of Wikipedias by featured](/wiki/Wikipedia_featured_articles "Wikipedia featured articles") and [good articles](/wiki/Wikipedia_good_articles "Wikipedia good articles") (both updated manually)
- [List of Wikipedias by creation date](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Anniversary "en:Wikipedia:Anniversary") (incomplete)
- [List of Wikipedias in multiple writing systems](/wiki/Wikipedias_in_multiple_writing_systems "Wikipedias in multiple writing systems")
- [List of Wikipedias having local media files](/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_having_local_media_files "List of Wikipedias having local media files") and [zero local media files](/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_having_zero_local_media_files "List of Wikipedias having zero local media files") (both updated manually)
- [List of Wikipedia milestones](/wiki/Wikipedia_milestones "Wikipedia milestones") or [en:Wikipedia:Milestone statistics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Milestone_statistics "en:Wikipedia:Milestone statistics") (tracking of major article-count milestones)
- [List of largest wikis](/wiki/List_of_largest_wikis "List of largest wikis") (not just Wikimedia wikis)
- [Wikimedia News](/wiki/Wikimedia_News "Wikimedia News") (announcements and tracking of milestones for all Wikimedia projects)
- [Tell us about your Wikipedia](/wiki/Tell_us_about_your_Wikipedia "Tell us about your Wikipedia")

## Notes

- The "All pages" column refers to the number of pages in all namespaces, including both articles (the [official article count](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Manual:Article_count "mw:Manual:Article count") of each wiki) and non-articles (user pages, images, talk pages, "project" pages, categories, and templates).
- "Active Users" are registered users who have made at least one edit in the last thirty days.
- "Files" is the number of locally uploaded files. Note that some large Wikipedias do not use local images or other media files and rely on [Commons](/wiki/Wikimedia_Commons "Wikimedia Commons") completely, so the value "0" is not a glitch (see also [List of Wikipedias having zero local media files](/wiki/List_of_Wikipedias_having_zero_local_media_files "List of Wikipedias having zero local media files")).

## All Wikipedias ordered by number of articles

The languages listed here are Wikipedias that have been created as separate subdomains of wikipedia.org, ordered by number of [articles](https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Manual:Article_count "mw:Manual:Article count"). The table can also be sorted by other columns. It excludes [closed Wikipedias](#Closed_and_read-only). Historical data of this table dating back to 2007 can be found in the [history of this table](https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_Wikipedias/Table&action=history) or, after 15 October 2022, in the [history of the current source of the data](https://commons.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Data:Wikipedia_statistics/data.tab&action=history).

These statistics are updated nine times a day. See [commons:Data:Wikipedia statistics/data.tab](https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Data:Wikipedia_statistics/data.tab "commons:Data:Wikipedia statistics/data.tab") for the date/time of last update. (If reloading this page doesn't update the numbers to what is seen at Commons, try [purging the cache](/wiki/Special:Purge/List_of_Wikipedias "Special:Purge/List of Wikipedias").)

## Other Wikipedias

### Not yet created

Please visit the [Wikimedia Incubator](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/ "incubator:") for new language versions (known as "tests") that may become stand-alone wikis in the future. See the Incubator [Manual](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Help:Manual "incubator:Help:Manual") and [FAQ](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Help:FAQ "incubator:Help:FAQ") for more information.

- [Manually maintained list of test Wikipedias](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Template:Tests/wp "incubator:Template:Tests/wp") in the Incubator
- [Search for a wiki](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Special:SearchWiki "incubator:Special:SearchWiki") in over 400 different languages (includes normal Wikipedias and test Wikipedias)

### Closed and read-only

These Wikipedias are closed and in read-only status. Existing users can still log in and their user preferences are still effective, but they cannot edit any pages. Editiable copies of these Wikipedias can be found in the Incubator; for example, the page [cho:Chahta](https://cho.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chahta "cho:Chahta") at the closed Choctaw Wikipedia can be found (and edited) at [incubator:Wp/cho/Chahta](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/cho/Chahta "incubator:Wp/cho/Chahta").

1. [aa:](https://aa.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "aa:") â€“ The [Afar](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afar_language "w:Afar language") Wikipedia was [closed on 10 May 2008](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Afar_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Afar Wikipedia"). It is now found at [incubator:Wp/aa](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/aa "incubator:Wp/aa").
2. [ak:](https://ak.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "ak:") â€“ The [Akan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Akan_language "w:Akan language") Wikipedia was [closed on 1 April 2023](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Akan_Wikipedia_2 "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Akan Wikipedia 2"). It should be noted that Akan is now considered a family of languages, so the ak.wikipedia domain has been split into two separate projects (and potentially more): one for [Twi](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twi "w:Twi") at [tw:](https://tw.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "tw:"), and another for [Fante](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fante_dialect "w:Fante dialect") at [fat:](https://fat.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "fat:").
3. [cr:](https://cr.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "cr:") - The [Cree](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cree "w:Cree") Wikipedia was [closed on 27 September 2025](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Cree_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Cree Wikipedia"). It is now found at [incubator:Wp/cr](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/cr "incubator:Wp/cr").
4. [cho:](https://cho.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "cho:") â€“ The [Choctaw](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Choctaw_language "w:Choctaw language") Wikipedia was [closed on 3 July 2007](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Choctaw_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Choctaw Wikipedia"), following a community vote. It is now found at [incubator:Wp/cho](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/cho "incubator:Wp/cho").
5. [ho:](https://ho.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "ho:") â€“ The [Hiri Motu](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hiri_Motu "w:Hiri Motu") Wikipedia was [closed on 9 July 2007](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Hiri_Motu_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Hiri Motu Wikipedia"). It is now found at [incubator:Wp/ho](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/ho "incubator:Wp/ho").
6. [hz:](https://hz.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "hz:") â€“ The [Herero](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herero_language "w:Herero language") Wikipedia was [closed on 24 July 2007](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Herero_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Herero Wikipedia"). The wiki has been emptied and locked, but the original user pages still exist. It is now re-incubated at [incubator:Wp/hz](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/hz "incubator:Wp/hz").
7. [ii:](https://ii.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "ii:") â€“ The [Sichuan Yi](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nuosu_language "w:Nuosu language") Wikipedia was [closed on 29 July 2007](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Yi_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Yi Wikipedia"). It is now found at [incubator:Wp/ii](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/ii "incubator:Wp/ii").
8. [kj:](https://kj.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "kj:") â€“ The [Kwanyama](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kwanyama "w:Kwanyama") Wikipedia was [closed on 10 July 2007](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Kwanyama_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Kwanyama Wikipedia"). It is now found at [incubator:Wp/kj](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/kj "incubator:Wp/kj").
9. [kl:](https://kl.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "kl:") - The [Kalaallisut](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greenlandic_language "w:Greenlandic language")/Greenlandic Wikipedia was [closed on 27 September 2025](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Greenlandic_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Greenlandic Wikipedia"). It is now found at [incubator:Wp/kl](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/kl "incubator:Wp/kl").
10. [kr:](https://kr.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "kr:") â€“ The [Kanuri](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kanuri_language "w:Kanuri language") Wikipedia was [closed on 3 May 2007](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Kanuri_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Kanuri Wikipedia"), following a community vote. The reason was the absence of both content and community. As Kanuri is considered as a macrolanguage, where member language codes of the macro has lack of mutual intelligibility, a [Central Kanuri](https://knc.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "knc:") (knc) Wikipedia was re-launched in 2025.
11. [lrc:](https://lrc.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "lrc:") â€“ The [Northern Luri](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_Luri_language "w:Northern Luri language") Wikipedia was [closed on 14 January 2021](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Northern_Luri_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Northern Luri Wikipedia"). As almost all of the former contents were confirmed not written in proper Luri, they were not imported back into the Incubator. Users who speak the language are encouraged to re-start [a test project](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/lrc "incubator:Wp/lrc").
12. [mh:](https://mh.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "mh:") â€“ The [Marshallese](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marshallese_language "w:Marshallese language") Wikipedia was [closed on 4 May 2008](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Marshallese_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Marshallese Wikipedia"). It is now found at [incubator:Wp/mh](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/mh "incubator:Wp/mh").
13. [mus:](https://mus.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "mus:") â€“ The [Muscogee](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muscogee_language "w:Muscogee language") Wikipedia was [closed on 10 July 2007](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Muscogee_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Muscogee Wikipedia"). It is now found at [incubator:Wp/mus](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/mus "incubator:Wp/mus").
14. [na:](https://na.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "na:") â€“ The [Nauruan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nauruan_language "w:Nauruan language") Wikipedia was [closed on 1 May 2023](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Nauruan_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Nauruan Wikipedia"). The contents of nawiki were imported into [Incubator Wp/na](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/na "incubator:Wp/na"), but deleted in 2025 due to a discussion that doubt the quality of imported-in contents; users who are familiar with speaking Nauruan are free to re-start such a project from scratch.
15. [ng:](https://ng.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "ng:") â€“ The [Ndonga](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ndonga "w:Ndonga") Wikipedia was [closed on 10 January 2010](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Ndonga_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Ndonga Wikipedia"). It is now found at [incubator:Wp/ng](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/ng "incubator:Wp/ng").
16. [pih:](https://pih.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "pih:") â€“ The [Pitkern](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pitkern "w:Pitkern") Wikipedia was [closed on 19 March 2025](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Pitkern_%26_Norfuk_Wikipedia_3 "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Pitkern & Norfuk Wikipedia 3"). Due to lack of useful contents, pages on pihwiki were not imported into Incubator; users who are familiar with speaking Pitkern are free to re-start [such a project](https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/pih "incubator:Wp/pih") from scratch.

See also our [Special:SiteMatrix](/wiki/Special:SiteMatrix "Special:SiteMatrix"), where the closed Wikipedias are crossed out (and the red links indicate wikis that have never existed). There is also a configuration file listing [all closed Wikimedia projects](https://noc.wikimedia.org/conf/highlight.php?file=dblists/closed.dblist).

### Deleted but hosted elsewhere

These Wikipedias are no longer hosted by Wikimedia. They have been moved to other hosts.

1. tlh â€“ The [Klingon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Klingon_language "w:Klingon language") Wikipedia was permanently locked in August 2005, and was moved to Wikia (Fandom) as the [Klingon Wiki](https://community.fandom.com/wiki/w:c:Klingon "wikia:Klingon"). For details, see the [history of the Klingon Wikipedia](/wiki/History_of_the_Klingon_Wikipedia "History of the Klingon Wikipedia").
2. ru-sib â€“ The [Siberian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Siberian_language "w:Siberian language") Wikipedia was [deleted in 2007](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Deletion_of_Siberian_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Deletion of Siberian Wikipedia") after it became apparent that the creation of the wiki in 2006 was based on a hoax. The wiki's content was moved to the [sibvolgota](http://yauzaforum.ru/upliner/sibvolgota/) ([archive link](https://web.archive.org/web/20121008014455/http://yauzaforum.ru/upliner/sibvolgota/index.php?title=%D0%93%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%BA%D0%B0)).
3. [mo:](https://mo.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "mo:") â€“ The [Moldovan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moldovan_language "w:Moldovan language") Wikipedia in the [Moldovan Cyrillic alphabet](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moldovan_Cyrillic_alphabet "w:Moldovan Cyrillic alphabet") was [deleted in November 2017](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Deletion_of_Moldovan_Wikipedia_2 "Proposals for closing projects/Deletion of Moldovan Wikipedia 2"), a decade after being [closed](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Moldovan_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Moldovan Wikipedia"). It is now hosted by Fandom as [Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºĞ¸Ğ¿ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ñ](https://wpmo.fandom.com/mo/wiki/ĞŸĞ°Ó‚Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°_Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ‡Ğ¸Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ»Ñ). The [mo:](https://mo.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "mo:") interlanguage prefix now points to the Romanian Wikipedia.

This list previously included the [Toki Pona](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Toki_Pona "w:Toki Pona") Wikipedia ([tok:](https://tok.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "tok:")), which was locked in 2004, [officially closed in 2008](/wiki/Proposals_for_closing_projects/Closure_of_Tokipona_Wikipedia "Proposals for closing projects/Closure of Tokipona Wikipedia"), and [deleted in 2010](https://phabricator.wikimedia.org/T13511 "phab:T13511") due to the lack of a valid ISO language code. After moving to Wikicities (later Wikia, then [Fandom](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fandom_(website) "w:Fandom (website)")) and thence to <https://wikipesija.org>, it [returned to Wikimedia servers in 2025](/wiki/Requests_for_new_languages/Wikipedia_Toki_Pona_2 "Requests for new languages/Wikipedia Toki Pona 2") after receiving an ISO code.

### Nonstandard language codes

These Wikipedias use language codes that do not conform to the [ISO 639](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_639 "w:ISO 639") standard (which is how wiki subdomains are chosen nowadays).

1. [als:](https://als.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "als:") â€“ originally used for the [Alsatian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alsatian_dialect "w:Alsatian dialect") Wikipedia, which now encompasses the [Alemannic dialects](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alemannic_German "w:Alemannic German") in general â€” the official code [gsw](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/gsw) is being considered as a replacement subdomain (note that [als](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/als) officially represents the unrelated language [Tosk Albanian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tosk_Albanian "w:Tosk Albanian"))
2. [bat-smg:](https://bat-smg.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "bat-smg:") â€“ invented code used for the [Samogitian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samogitian_language "w:Samogitian language") Wikipedia (not the official code [sgs](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/sgs))
3. [be-tarask:](https://be-tarask.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "be-tarask:") â€“ invented code used for the [Belarusian (TaraÅ¡kievica)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tara%C5%A1kievica "w:TaraÅ¡kievica") Wikipedia, combination of be for Belarusian and IETF language tag tarask for TaraÅ¡kievica
4. [bh:](https://bh.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "bh:") - deprecated code used for the [Bhojpuri](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bhojpuri_language "w:Bhojpuri language") Wikipedia (bh is the deprecated ISO 639-1 code for the [Bihari languages](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bihari_languages "w:Bihari languages"), which Bhojpuri is a part of. The official code for Bhojpuri is [bho](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/bho))
5. [cbk-zam:](https://cbk-zam.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "cbk-zam:") â€“ invented code used for the [Zamboanga Chavacano](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chavacano "w:Chavacano") Wikipedia (note that [cbk](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/cbk) is the correct code for the larger family of langugages Zamboanga Chavacano is a member of)
6. [fiu-vro:](https://fiu-vro.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "fiu-vro:") â€“ invented code used for the [VÃµro](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/V%C3%B5ro_language "w:VÃµro language") Wikipedia (not the official code [vro](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/vro) â€” note that [fiu](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/fiu) is the official code for the family of languages VÃµro is a member of)
7. [ksh:](https://ksh.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "ksh:") â€“ code used for the [Ripuarian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ripuarian_language "w:Ripuarian language") Wikipedia, even though [ksh](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/ksh) actually represents [KÃ¶lsch (or Colognian)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colognian "w:Colognian"), a subset of Ripuarian
8. [map-bms:](https://map-bms.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "map-bms:") â€“ invented code used for the [Banyumasan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Banyumasan_dialect "w:Banyumasan dialect") Wikipedia (note that [map](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/map) does represent the family of languages the Banyumasan dialect falls within)
9. [nds-nl:](https://nds-nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "nds-nl:") â€“ invented code used for [Dutch Low Saxon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_Low_Saxon "w:Dutch Low Saxon") Wikipedia would technically be the correct code for Low Saxon spoken in the Netherlands (i.e., nds-NL), but is therefore redundant with [nds:](https://nds.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "nds:"), the code used for the [Low German/Low Saxon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German "w:Low German") Wikipedia (note that [nds](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/nds) is the correct code for the Low German/Low Saxon family of languages, which Dutch Low Saxon is a member of)
10. [nrm:](https://nrm.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "nrm:") â€“ code used for the [Norman](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norman_language "w:Norman language") Wikipedia (not the official code [nrf](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/nrf) â€” note that [nrm](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/nrm) is the official code for the completely unrelated language [Narom](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Narom_language "w:Narom language"))
11. [roa-rup:](https://roa-rup.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "roa-rup:") â€“ invented code used for the [Aromanian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aromanian_language "w:Aromanian language") Wikipedia (not the official code [rup](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/rup) â€” note that [roa](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/roa) is the standard code for the larger family of Romance languages that Aromanian is a member of)
12. [roa-tara:](https://roa-tara.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "roa-tara:") â€“ invented code used for the [Tarantino](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tarantino_dialect "w:Tarantino dialect") Wikipedia (again, [roa](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/roa) is the standard code for the large family of Romance languages that the Tarantino dialect falls within)
13. [sh:](https://sh.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "sh:") â€“ deprecated code used for the [Serbo-Croatian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian "w:Serbo-Croatian") Wikipedia (not the official code [hbs](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/hbs))
14. [simple:](https://simple.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "simple:") â€“ invented code used for the Simple [English](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language "w:English language") Wikipedia (which is just an IETF language tag, not the formal code en-simple)
15. [zh-classical:](https://zh-classical.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "zh-classical:") â€“ invented code used for the [Classical Chinese](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Chinese "w:Classical Chinese") Wikipedia (not the official code [lzh](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/lzh))
16. [zh-min-nan:](https://zh-min-nan.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "zh-min-nan:") â€“ invented code used for the [Southern Min](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min "w:Southern Min") Wikipedia (not the official code [nan](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/nan))
17. [zh-yue:](https://zh-yue.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "zh-yue:") â€“ invented code used for the [Cantonese](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese "w:Cantonese") Wikipedia (not the official code [yue](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/yue))

Note that [renaming wiki subdomains is very difficult](https://phabricator.wikimedia.org/T172035 "phab:T172035"), which is why so many of these nonstandard codes are still in use despite the existence of alternatives.

### Redirects

1. [be-x-old:](https://be-tarask.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "be-x-old:") â€“ redirects to [be-tarask:](https://be-tarask.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "be-tarask:") (see above section)
2. [cz:](https://cs.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "cz:") â€“ redirects to [cs:](https://cs.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "cs:") (the [Czech](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language "w:Czech language") Wikipedia)
3. [dk:](https://da.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "dk:") â€“ redirects to [da:](https://da.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "da:") (the [Danish](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language "w:Danish language") Wikipedia)
4. [jp:](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "jp:") â€“ redirects to [ja:](https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "ja:") (the [Japanese](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language "w:Japanese language") Wikipedia)
5. [mo:](https://mo.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "mo:") â€“ redirects to [ro:](https://ro.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "ro:") (as discussed [above](#Deleted_Wikipedias_now_hosted_elsewhere), the [Moldovan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moldovan_language "w:Moldovan language") Wikipedia now redirects to the [Romanian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romanian_language "w:Romanian language") Wikipedia)
6. [nan:](https://zh-min-nan.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "nan:") â€“ redirects to [zh-min-nan:](https://zh-min-nan.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "zh-min-nan:") (the [Southern Min](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min "w:Southern Min") Wikipedia)
7. [nb:](https://no.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "nb:") â€“ redirects to [no:](https://no.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "no:") (the [Norwegian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language "w:Norwegian language") Wikipedia using [BokmÃ¥l orthography](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bokm%C3%A5l "w:BokmÃ¥l"))
8. [yue:](https://zh-yue.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "yue:") â€“ redirects to [zh-yue:](https://zh-yue.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "zh-yue:") (the [Cantonese](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese "w:Cantonese") Wikipedia)

### Non-language subdomains

- [nostalgia:](https://nostalgia.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "nostalgia:") (alias: [nost:](https://nostalgia.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "nost:")) â€“ A read-only snapshot of English Wikipedia's early days.
- [sep11:](//meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Sep11wiki "sep11:") â€“ The [Sep11wiki](/wiki/Sep11wiki "Sep11wiki") existed with a .wikipedia.org URL from 2001 to 2008, despite its totally different scope and purpose from all other Wikipedias. It was made read-only in 2006 and closed two years later.
- [ten:](https://ten.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "tenwiki:") â€“ Used for [Wikipedia 10](/wiki/Wikipedia_10 "Wikipedia 10"), the 10th anniversary of Wikipedia celebration events. (Since "[ten](https://iso639-3.sil.org/code/ten "iso639-3:ten")" is an ISO language code for the extinct [Tama language in Colombia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tama_language_(Colombia) "w:Tama language (Colombia)"), the interwiki prefix "[tenwiki:](https://ten.wikipedia.org/wiki/ "tenwiki:")" is now used to refer to this site.)

- [Special:SiteMatrix](/wiki/Special:SiteMatrix "Special:SiteMatrix") â€“ automatically generated table of languages for all projects (including wikis not yet created), ordered by language code
- [Template:Active Wikipedias](/wiki/Template:Active_Wikipedias "Template:Active Wikipedias") â€“ just a list of all existing Wikipedias (with links) ordered by local language name

- [Wikipedia logo in each language](/wiki/Wikipedia_logo_in_each_language "Wikipedia logo in each language"), including the name "Wikipedia" in different languages

## Thank you for supporting Wikipedia today!

For 25 years, Wikipedia has been an oasis of free and collaborative informationâ€”driven by people, not profit. You are one of the rare 2% of readers who donate to keep it thriving. Thank youâ€”your gift makes a difference.

The Wikimedia Foundation sustains Wikipedia, and is recognized as a highly effective and efficient nonprofit.

## Where your donation goes

[[edit](/w/index.php?title=Template:Infobox/Default/en&action=edit&section=T-1 "Edit section: Where your donation goes")]

Technology: Servers, bandwidth, maintenance, development. Wikipedia is one of the top 10 websites in the world, and it runs on a fraction of what other top websites spend.

People and Projects: The other top websites have thousands of employees. Wikimedia Foundation has about 700 staff and contractors to support a wide variety of projects, making your donation a great investment in a highly-efficient not-for-profit organization.

[Tax deductibility information](https://donate.wikimedia.org/wiki/Special:LandingCheck?landing_page=Tax_deductibility&basic=true&language=en)

We do not sell or trade your information to anyone. By donating, you agree to share your personal information with the Wikimedia Foundation, the nonprofit organization that hosts Wikipedia and other Wikimedia projects, and its service providers pursuant to our [donor policy](https://foundation.wikimedia.org/wiki/Special:LandingCheck?landing_page=Donor_privacy_policy&basic=true&language=en). Wikimedia Foundation and its service providers are located in the United States and in other countries whose privacy laws may not be equivalent to your own. For more information please read our [donor policy](https://foundation.wikimedia.org/wiki/Special:LandingCheck?landing_page=Donor_privacy_policy&basic=true&language=en).

For recurring donors, fixed monthly payments will be debited by the Wikimedia Foundation on the monthly anniversary of the first donation, until such time as you notify us to discontinue them. Donations initiated on the 29, 30, or 31 of the month will recur on the last day of the month for shorter months, as close to the original date as possible. For questions, please contact donate@wikimedia.org.

- [Problems donating?](https://donate.wikimedia.org/wiki/Special:LandingCheck?landing_page=Problems_donating&basic=true&language=en)
- [Other ways to give](https://wikimediafoundation.org/en/give/#ways-to-give)
- [Frequently asked questions](https://donate.wikimedia.org/wiki/Special:LandingCheck?landing_page=FAQ&basic=true&language=en)

Monthly support is the best way to ensure that Wikipedia keeps thriving.

(Redirected from [List of Wikipedia mobile applications](/w/index.php?title=List_of_Wikipedia_mobile_applications&redirect=no "List of Wikipedia mobile applications"))WikipediaScreenshot
Official Wikipedia app for [iOS](/wiki/IOS "IOS")[Developer](/wiki/Programmer "Programmer")[Wikimedia Foundation](/wiki/Wikimedia_Foundation "Wikimedia Foundation")[Repository](/wiki/Repository_(version_control) "Repository (version control)")

- [Android](https://github.com/wikimedia/apps-android-wikipedia)
- [iOS](https://github.com/wikimedia/wikipedia-ios)

Written in[Kotlin](/wiki/Kotlin_(programming_language) "Kotlin (programming language)")Website[doc.wikimedia.org](https://doc.wikimedia.org/#apps)

A number of organizations within the [Wikimedia movement](/wiki/Wikimedia_movement "Wikimedia movement") including the [Wikimedia Foundation](/wiki/Wikimedia_Foundation "Wikimedia Foundation") publish official [mobile apps](/wiki/Mobile_app "Mobile app") for [mobile access](/wiki/Wikipedia:Mobile_access "Wikipedia:Mobile access") to [Wikipedia](/wiki/Wikipedia "Wikipedia"). All are available via the appropriate [app store](/wiki/App_store "App store") (e.g. [Google Play](/wiki/Google_Play "Google Play"), [App Store](/wiki/App_Store_(iOS) "App Store (iOS)"), [Microsoft Store](/wiki/Microsoft_Store "Microsoft Store"), [F-Droid](/wiki/F-Droid "F-Droid")). They can also be downloaded independently of any third-party store from the Wikimedia Foundation's releases website, which also keeps old and [beta versions](/wiki/Beta_(software) "Beta (software)").[[1]](#cite_note-1)

## Official apps

### Wikimedia Foundation

Wikipedia apps from the Wikimedia Foundation are called "Wikipedia".

Android

The [Android](/wiki/Android_(operating_system) "Android (operating system)") app allows users to read and edit articles directly from the app.[[2]](#cite_note-2) It is available on [Play Store](/wiki/Play_Store "Play Store"), [Galaxy Store](/wiki/Samsung_Galaxy_Store "Samsung Galaxy Store"),[[3]](#cite_note-3) [Aptoide](/wiki/Aptoide "Aptoide"),[[4]](#cite_note-4) [Cafe Bazaar](/wiki/Cafe_Bazaar "Cafe Bazaar"),[[5]](#cite_note-5) [F-Droid](/wiki/F-Droid "F-Droid"),[[6]](#cite_note-6) and [GetJar](/wiki/GetJar "GetJar").[[7]](#cite_note-7)
A separate app on the Play Store provides access to [beta](/wiki/Beta_(software_development) "Beta (software development)") features that may not be available in the standard Wikipedia app.[[8]](#cite_note-8)

In June 2025, a quiz game called Which Came First? was introduced to the app, which allows users to answer five questions regarding which historical event of two given events occurred first.[[9]](#cite_note-9)[[10]](#cite_note-10) A feature called Year in Review that allows users to see the time and topics they spent reading for a given year was also introduced that year.[[11]](#cite_note-11)

iOS

The [iOS](/wiki/IOS "IOS") app also allows users to read and edit articles directly from the app,[[12]](#cite_note-12)[[13]](#cite_note-13) similar to the Android app and [mobile web version](/wiki/Help:Mobile_access "Help:Mobile access"). It allows users to share an article via Facebook and other social websites, and to find [geotagged](/wiki/Geotagging "Geotagging") articles near their current location.[[14]](#cite_note-14) It does not allow users to see categories or see the normal desktop version.[[citation needed](/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed "Wikipedia:Citation needed")]

Windows

The [Metro-style app](/wiki/Metro-style_app "Metro-style app") provides a read-only version of Wikipedia, similar to the mobile web version. The app when used in [Windows RT](/wiki/Windows_RT "Windows RT") is incapable of showing [moving pictures](/wiki/GIF "GIF").[[citation needed](/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed "Wikipedia:Citation needed")]

KaiOS

The [KaiOS](/wiki/KaiOS "KaiOS") app was released in April 2024.[[15]](#cite_note-15)

### Kiwix

Kiwix has developed a number of offline apps based on Wikipedia content.

## Unassociated apps

These apps were mainly developed to display articles and are often used on platforms for which an official Wikipedia app was not formerly available, such as [Windows Phone](/wiki/Windows_Phone "Windows Phone"). Typical features include searching for articles, [bookmarks](/wiki/Bookmark_(World_Wide_Web) "Bookmark (World Wide Web)"), sharing, or enlarging [images](/wiki/Image "Image").[[citation needed](/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed "Wikipedia:Citation needed")]

Available
[Open source](/wiki/Open_source_software "Open source software")
[WikiNodes](/wiki/WikiNodes "WikiNodes")
By [Institute for Dynamic Educational Advancement](/wiki/Institute_for_Dynamic_Educational_Advancement "Institute for Dynamic Educational Advancement") (IDEA)[[16]](#cite_note-16)[[17]](#cite_note-17)[[18]](#cite_note-18)
No
[yes](https://web.archive.org/web/20110527140210/http://itunes.apple.com/us/app/wikinodes/id433834594)
[Wikiwand](/wiki/Wikiwand "Wikiwand")
Made to allow easier navigation and search than the website or the site's own app[[19]](#cite_note-19)[[20]](#cite_note-20)[[21]](#cite_note-21)
Currently invitation only[[22]](#cite_note-22)
[yes](https://web.archive.org/web/20150317223403/https://itunes.apple.com/app/wikiwand-faster-wikipedia-reader/id947444965)
Wikiweb
Wikiweb is a Wikipedia reader for iPhone and iPad that visualizes the connections between articles.[[23]](#cite_note-23)[[24]](#cite_note-24)
[yes](https://web.archive.org/web/20150621012222/https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/wikiweb-visual-wikipedia-reader/id499345601)
TripEnhancer
TripEnhancer is a Wikipedia reader for Android that reads aloud articles in the surroundings of the user.[[25]](#cite_note-25)
[yes](https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.naxx.tripenhancer.free)

## Related apps

There is an Android app for [Wikimedia Commons](/wiki/Wikimedia_Commons "Wikimedia Commons"), which is [community maintained](https://github.com/commons-app/apps-android-commons) and described on the [Commons mobile app page](https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Commons:Mobile_app "commons:Commons:Mobile app"). There was also an Android app for [Wiktionary](/wiki/Wiktionary "Wiktionary"), although it is no longer available.[[26]](#cite_note-26)


- [Help:Mobile access](/wiki/Help:Mobile_access "Help:Mobile access")

# Wikipedia

[Wikimedia Foundation](/store/apps/dev?id=6169333749249604352)4.4star695K reviews50M+DownloadsEveryoneinfoInstallShareAdd to wishlistplay_arrowTrailer

## About this app

arrow_forwardThe best Wikipedia experience on your Mobile device. Ad-free and free of charge, forever. With the official Wikipedia app, you can search and explore 40+ million articles in 300+ languages, no matter where you are.== Why you'll love the this app ==1. It's free and openWikipedia is the encyclopedia that anyone can edit. Articles on Wikipedia are freely licensed and the app code is 100% open source. The heart and soul of Wikipedia is a community of people working to bring you unlimited access to free, reliable and neutral information.2. No adsWikipedia is a place to learn, not a place for advertising. This app is made by the Wikimedia Foundation, a nonprofit organization that supports and operates Wikipedia. We provide this service in the pursuit of open knowledge thatâ€™s always ad-free and never tracks your data. 3. Read in your languageSearch 40 million articles in over 300 languages in the worldâ€™s largest source of information. Set your preferred languages in the app and easily switch between them when browsing or reading. 4. Use it offlineSave your favorite articles and read Wikipedia offline with â€œMy listsâ€œ. Name lists as you like and collect articles across different languages. Saved articles and reading lists are synced across all your devices and are available even when you do not have internet connectivity.5. Attention to detail and night modeThe app embraces Wikipediaâ€™s simplicity and adds delight to it. A beautiful and distraction-free interface lets you focus on the essential: reading articles. With text size adjustment and themes in pure black, dark, sepia or light, you can choose the most pleasant reading experience for you.== Broaden your horizon with these features == 1. Customize your Explore feed"Explore" lets you see recommended Wikipedia content including current events, popular articles, captivating freely-licensed photos, events on this day in history, suggested articles based on your reading history, and more.2. Find and search Quickly find what you're looking for by searching within articles or with the search bar at the top of the app. You can even search using your favorite emojis or voice-enabled search.== We'd love your feedback ==1. To send feedback from the app: In the menu, press "Settings", then, in the "About" section, tap "Send app feedback".2. If you have experience with Java and the Android SDK, then we look forward to your contributions! More info: https://mediawiki.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Apps/Team/Android/App_hacking 3. Explanation of permissions needed by the app: https://mediawiki.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Apps/Android_FAQ#Security_and_Permissions 4. Privacy policy: https://m.wikimediafoundation.org/wiki/Privacy_policy 5. Terms of Use: https://m.wikimediafoundation.org/wiki/Terms_of_Use 6. About the Wikimedia Foundation:The Wikimedia Foundation is a charitable nonprofit organization that supports and operates Wikipedia and the other Wiki projects. It is funded mainly through donations. For more information, please visit our website: https://wikimediafoundation.org/Updated onDec 11, 2025Books & Reference

April 6, 2025Love the app! Honestly, I probably am using Wikipedia more than my web browser or reading articles from Google. Only one small issue I found: when in dark mode, the captions under images is a dark gray instead of the white like the rest of the article text. This makes it virtually impossible to see. Doesn't matter what article, if there's an in-line image, there's a barely readable, gray caption underneath if.237 people found this review helpfulDid you find this helpful?YesNoA Google usermore_vert

- Show review history

October 29, 2018This is such a great, well made app. It's probably my favorite app on my phone right now. You can create reading lists of different subjects and they are available offline. Furthermore, when reading an article and clicking on a highlighted word it gives a summary overlay popup that doesn't pull you away from the current article, however you can go to the full article if you desire to. This app and wikipedia in general are one of the silver linings of the attrocious noise the internet and apps have become.329 people found this review helpfulDid you find this helpful?YesNoNed Crooksmore_vert

iPhone, iPad, iMessage

Wikipedia: Free knowledge without ads, always at your fingertips
The official Wikipedia app for iOS helps you explore the worldâ€™s largest free knowledge project â€” ad-free and free of charge, forever. With 60+ million articles in nearly 300 languages, your favorite encyclopedia is always at your fingertips.
Why youâ€™ll love this app
Free, open, and ad-free
Wikipedia is written and verified by volunteers worldwide, supported by the nonprofit Wikimedia Foundation. No ads, no tracking â€” just knowledge you can trust.
Search smarter, discover more
Find the information you need without distraction. Search across 300 languages, explore trending and breaking news through a personalized feed.
Add knowledge to your Home Screen
Use widgets for quick access to trending articles, featured content, or the â€œPicture of the Day,â€ right from your Home Screen.
Read your way
Choose from light, sepia, dark, or pure black themes. Adjust text size and image dimming for comfortable reading anytime, anywhere.
Explore nearby places
Learn about landmarks and locations near you â€” or places you dream of visiting â€” through map-based article discovery.
Stay connected offline
Save articles to custom reading lists and access them offline â€” perfect for travel or learning without internet access.
Share and continue seamlessly
Share articles and images with friends, or use Handoff to keep reading across your Apple devices.
Get insights into your activity
See your own reading and contribution activity on Wikipedia with personalized insights that help you understand and celebrate how you use engage with Wikipedia.
Stay organized with tabs
Open multiple articles in tabs and switch between them with ease, just like in a browser. Compare topics, keep your place, and dive deeper without losing track.
Join the conversation
Read and reply to article discussion pages, and get notifications when discussions you follow are updated.
Contribute on the go
Manage your Watchlist to help keep Wikipedia accurate and up to date.
Additional Information
Feedback: In the app, go to Settings â†’ Send app feedback.
Contribute to translations: https://translatewiki.net/wiki/Translating:WikimediaMobile

- ### Fantastic app with one major glitch

03/20/2022

triple7marc

First of all, I love this app. It is very professionally made. The UI is clean and intuitive. Links work how youâ€™d expect them to, itâ€™s easy to search, navigate through pages and find words within articles. But there is one major glitch that makes me extremely frustrated - editing documents. For some reason the cursor is virtually unusable when editing documents. It jumps around and sometimes just gets stuck in place making it impossible to set it where you want to begin typing. There are other problems with it that I wonâ€™t get into but really the only flaw of this app id the editing UI. This app would be absolutely PERFECT if that is fixed.But if you donâ€™t edit pages like I do, youâ€™ll absolutely love this app! Think of all the FREE information youâ€™re getting from this app. Truly mind-boggling the world that we live in.

When I found out all of this was translated into an app, I was joyous (as weird as that sounds lol). Now when Iâ€™m traveling, or eating, or seriously whenever I have free time, I just get on this app and start reading. Itâ€™s very easy to use (keep in mind that I am a reader, not an editor so I do not have an editorâ€™s experience with this app). The interface is quite lovely, giving customization options in order to fit individual reading preferences. It really is a privilege to live in a society where information can be so accessible, especially thanks to Wikipedia who preaches the ethics of information being free and in anybodyâ€™s disposal. My immigrant mother who is still learning English appreciates the Spanish accessibility as well! Itâ€™s just an amazing app, and I would 100% recommend it to anybody. The world is at our fingertips, why not?

- ### Wow itâ€™s even worse than the UI Update to the Desktop Website

08/03/2023

took the name I wanted

I will never understand why â€œmobile-optimizedâ€ or â€œmobile-firstâ€ means a terrible, unusable experience. I was hoping the app would have an easy way of selecting the Vector skin by default for Wikipedia pagesâ€”you know, the way the website used to normally look for the past 10 years before the terrible â€œmobileâ€ update they rolled out. Currently the only way to view Wikipedia is to manually add ?useskin=vector to the end of ever url. What a pain. Or make an account, which I never had to and shouldnâ€™t have to do. But gee, I didnâ€™t know when I was better off! The app is so bad, with a fixed table of contents margin on the left third of the screen, it makes the website look good by comparison. No way to select what skin you want, in fact, youâ€™re stuck between blinding white light mode or pitch black dark mode. Another typical disastrous design choice, Why canâ€™t anybody make a neutral color that is easy on the eyes day or night anymore?And donâ€™t expect an easy way to read on a tablet/iPad. This version requires constant scrolling to read anything. Instantly deleted. Better off sticking with viewing pages in a web browser.


# Wow itâ€™s even worse than the UI Update to the Desktop Website


- ### The mobile app, is somehow worse than the mobile site

04/09/2020

floofysheep

After writing this, i will have deleted the app in favour of the website. This is for one reason: convenience, its way easier to find and go to a specific part of an article on the site rather then the app. Letâ€™s use the page on, Visby Sweden as an example. On the website, when you scroll down below the general information, you get headers like: â€œetymologyâ€, â€œhistoryâ€, â€œclimateâ€, and â€œinfrastructureâ€, you can then tap on one or more of these things to open that/those specific section(s). On the app, you cannot do this. Letâ€™s say i want to get to the â€œinfrastructureâ€ section, i now have to scroll down through the â€œetymologyâ€ through â€œclimateâ€ sections of the article just to get to the section I want to read. Why, why isnâ€™t the app like the mobile version of the website? I have checked the settings to see if this was something i had to turn on, I couldnâ€™t find it, either i am missing something (if so deepest apologies) or this simple feature doesnâ€™t exist.Kindest regards - Fluffysheep

On the app we provide a table of contents which allows you to see and navigate to any section of the article. It is available via the button in the lower left of every article.

# Version History

- This update includes an A/B test of our new Activity tab. The tab surfaces recent reading activity, including time spent, articles viewed, saved items, and edits. All insights are generated locally on your device, ensuring your data remains private.

7.8.8 Dec 15

7.8.7 Dec 12
- Minor updates and enhancements

7.8.6 Nov 27

7.8.5 Nov 10
- This release contains tests within the tabbed browsing feature for select users. Weâ€™re exploring different experiences for what happens when you open a new tab, providing recommendations for articles based on your recent tabs, and providing a way to close all tabs at once.
We also fixed a bug that was affecting Search within the "Saved" tab.

7.8.4 Oct 27
- Minor updates and enhancements.

7.8.3 Sep 29

7.8.2 Sep 15

7.8.1 Sep 1

7.8.0 Aug 6
- Big news: Tabs have arrived!
The wait is over. Browsing with tabs has officially landed on iOS.
â€¢ Open now, read later: Long-press links to open them in a new tab or in the background.
â€¢ Jump between articles: Quickly switch between everything youâ€™re reading with the new tabs overview.
â€¢ Never lose your place: Tabs remember exactly where you left off in the article
We've also improved the toolbar navigation on iPad! Easily switch from articles to the main view by tapping an item in the top toolbar.
Thanks for using the Wikipedia app. Happy reading!

7.7.8 Jul 22

7.7.7 Jun 27
- This update brings a few exciting changes to your Wikipedia experience:
â€¢ New Article Search Bar: We've introduced a redesigned article search bar, now available to all users.
â€¢ Tabbed Browsing (A/B Test): We're testing a new tabbed browsing feature with a subset of users in select countries, specifically on the Arabic, English, and Japanese Wikipedias. This allows for easier switching between multiple open articles. We plan to roll out tabbed browsing more broadly later this year.
As always, thank you for using the Wikipedia app!

7.7.6 Jun 12
- This release includes on-device statistics improvements for future â€œWikipedia Year in Reviewâ€ features. We also began a short test on Turkish, Spanish, French, and Chinese Wikipedias to explore the concept of an Activity tab.

7.7.5 May 6
- â€¢ We added support for Temporary Accounts to Wikipedias where they are currently enabled, to protect the IP addresses of unregistered editors.
â€¢ With the help of volunteer developers, we fixed several bugs
â€¢ The â€œadd a linkâ€ editing flow was not automatically searching the text
â€¢ The keyboard was occasionally covering input fields within â€œAdd an imageâ€ editing flow
â€¢ The search cursor was sometimes not active upon first tap
â€¢ Date formatting on talk pages was not matching device settings

7.7.4 Apr 23

7.7.3 Apr 17

7.7.2 Mar 3
- Whatâ€™s new:
â€¢ Access the Profile menu has now been added to Saved, Search, Places, and History
â€¢ Thanks to volunteer developer support, several bugs were fixed.
â€¢ On Arabic, French, German, and Japanese Wikipedias, we are testing a more prominent search bar within the article view
Have feedback? Feel free to reach out to iOS-support@wikimedia.org!

7.7.1 Feb 13
- We made improvements to update the look and feel of the navigation across the app.

7.7.0 Jan 30

7.6.4 Jan 21
- Look back on 2024 through the lens of Wikipedia with Year in Review! See insights about which articles we read and the edits we made.

7.6.3 Jan 15
- An experimental â€œWikipedia Year in Reviewâ€ feature was added for users in Italy and Mexico.

7.6.2 11/22/2024

7.6.1 10/23/2024
- In this release, we introduced a profile menu to our app navigation. Profile gives you quick access to Watchlist, Notifications, Talk Page, and more while reading an article.

7.6.0 10/08/2024
- Multiple enhancements and bug fixes were completed in collaboration with volunteer developers.

7.5.9 09/23/2024
- In this release, we made bug fixes and improvements, and began a short A/B test in select languages.
â€¢ We fixed a bug that was causing the app to crash in some settings after opening revision history, watchlist, or notifications center.
â€¢ We fixed a bug that was affecting the interface for adding images and links while editing.
â€¢ We launched two A/B tests for editors on Spanish, Portuguese, French, and Chinese Wikipedias that will prompt editors to add alternative text to images after they have completed a relevant edit.

7.5.8 09/03/2024

This update includes an A/B test of our new Activity tab. The tab surfaces recent reading activity, including time spent, articles viewed, saved items, and edits. All insights are generated locally on your device, ensuring your data remains private.

Picture of the day
[Pirogue](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pirogue "w:Pirogue") running on the [Mekong](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mekong "w:Mekong") in front of an island hosting a [Samanea saman](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samanea_saman "w:Samanea saman") (rain tree) and other trees, at sunset with pink clouds, seen from [Don Det](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Don_Det "w:Don Det"), [Si Phan Don](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Si_Phan_Don "w:Si Phan Don"), Laos.

- [RSS feed](https://commons.wikimedia.org/w/api.php?action=featuredfeed&feed=potd&feedformat=rss&language=en)
- [Subscribe](https://lists.wikimedia.org/mailman/listinfo/daily-image-l)
- [Previous Pictures of the day](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Commons:Picture_of_the_day "Special:MyLanguage/Commons:Picture of the day")

A [FPV video](/wiki/Category:First-person_videos_on_foot "Category:First-person videos on foot") of walking in [Novi Sad, Serbia](/wiki/Category:Novi_Sad "Category:Novi Sad")[Problems playing the file?](/wiki/Commons:Media_help "Commons:Media help")

Participating
[LogÂ in](/wiki/Special:UserLogin "Special:UserLogin") [CreateÂ account](/wiki/Special:UserLogin/signup "Special:UserLogin/signup")
Browsing?
Please use the search box at the top of this page or [the links to the right](#Content)[the links further down](#Content). Feel free to subscribe to our [syndicated feeds](/wiki/Commons:Feeds "Commons:Feeds").
Using?
To fulfill the free license requirements, please read our [Reuse](/wiki/Commons:Reusing_content_outside_Wikimedia "Commons:Reusing content outside Wikimedia") guide. You can also [request a file](/wiki/Commons:File_requests "Commons:File requests") or [request permission for a file already on the internet](/wiki/Commons:Permission_requests "Commons:Permission requests").
Identifying?
Have a browse through [Category:Unidentified subjects](/wiki/Category:Unidentified_subjects "Category:Unidentified subjects"). If you find something you can identify, adjust the file's categories and [depicts](https://www.wikidata.org/wiki/Property:P180 "d:Property:P180") statements in [structured data](/wiki/Commons:Structured_data "Commons:Structured data").
Creating?
Check out all you need to know at our [Contributing your own work](/wiki/Commons:Contributing_your_own_work "Commons:Contributing your own work") guide.
and more!
Discussion?
See the [list of discussion pages](/wiki/Commons:Discussion_pages "Commons:Discussion pages").
To explore more ways you can contribute to this project, check out the [Community Portal](/wiki/Commons:Community_portal "Commons:Community portal").
Wiki Science Competition
Upload your photographs related to science for the Wiki Science Competition 2025. [Learn more about the contest!](/wiki/Commons:Wiki_Science_Competition_2025 "Commons:Wiki Science Competition 2025")
Monthly photo challenge
Take some photos and upload them to meet our monthly thematic challenge, get inspiration and try new subjects! [Learn more about the challenges!](/wiki/Commons:Photo_challenge "Commons:Photo challenge") [Check out this month's challenges](/wiki/Commons:Photo_challenge#Challenges_open_for_submission "Commons:Photo challenge")
Highlights

If you are browsing Commons for the first time, you may want to start with [Featured pictures](/wiki/Commons:Featured_pictures "Commons:Featured pictures"), [Quality images](/wiki/Commons:Quality_images "Commons:Quality images"), [Valued images](/wiki/Commons:Valued_images "Commons:Valued images") or [Featured media](/wiki/Commons:Featured_media "Commons:Featured media").You can also see some work created by our highly skilled contributors in [Meet our photographers](/wiki/Commons:Meet_our_photographers "Commons:Meet our photographers") and [Meet our illustrators](/wiki/Commons:Meet_our_illustrators "Commons:Meet our illustrators"). You may also be interested in [Picture of the Year](/wiki/Commons:Picture_of_the_Year "Commons:Picture of the Year").

From Wikidata

Welcome to Wikidata

the [free](https://foundation.wikimedia.org/wiki/Terms_of_Use "wmf:Terms of Use") knowledge base with [120,101,428](/wiki/Special:Statistics "Special:Statistics")Â dataÂ [items](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:Items "Special:MyLanguage/Help:Items") that [anyoneÂ canÂ edit](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Contribute "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Contribute").

[Introduction](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Introduction "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Introduction") â€¢ [Project Chat](/wiki/Wikidata:Project_chat "Wikidata:Project chat") â€¢ [Community Portal](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Community_portal "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Community portal") â€¢ [Help](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:Contents "Special:MyLanguage/Help:Contents")

Want to help translate? [Translate the missing messages](https://www.wikidata.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Translate&group=agg-Main_Page&filter=%21translated&action=page).

Welcome!

Wikidata is a free and open knowledge base that can be read and edited by both humans and machines.

Wikidata acts as central storage for the structured data of its Wikimedia sister projects including Wikipedia, Wikivoyage, Wiktionary, Wikisource, and others.

Wikidata also provides support to many other sites and services beyond just Wikimedia projects! The content of Wikidata is [available under a free license](https://creativecommons.org/publicdomain/zero/1.0/), [exported using standard formats](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Database_download "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Database download"), and [can be interlinked to other open data sets](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Data_access "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Data access") on the linked data web.

Get involvedFor a complete startersâ€™ guide, visit the [community portal](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Community_portal "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Community portal").

Learn about Wikidata

- What is Wikidata? Read the [Wikidata introduction](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Introduction "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Introduction").
- Explore Wikidata by looking at a featured showcase item for author [Douglas Adams (Q42)](/wiki/Q42 "Q42").
- Get started with Wikidata's [SPARQL query service](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:SPARQL_query_service/Wikidata_Query_Help "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:SPARQL query service/Wikidata Query Help").

Contribute to Wikidata

- Learn to edit Wikidata: follow the [tutorials](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Tours "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Tours").
- Work with other volunteers on a subject that interests you: [join a WikiProject](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:WikiProjects "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:WikiProjects").
- Individuals and organizations can also [donate data](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Data_donation "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Data donation").

Meet the Wikidata community

- Visit the [community portal](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Community_portal "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Community portal") or attend a [Wikidata event](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Events "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Events").
- Create a [user account](/wiki/Special:CreateAccount "Special:CreateAccount").
- Talk and ask questions on the [Project chat](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Project_chat "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Project chat"), [Telegram groups](https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Telegram#Wikidata "meta:Special:MyLanguage/Telegram"), or the [live IRC chat](irc://irc.libera.chat/wikidata)[connect](https://web.libera.chat/?channel=#wikidata).

Use data from Wikidata

- Learn how you can [retrieve and use data from Wikidata](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Data_access "Special:MyLanguage/Wikidata:Data access").

News

- 2025-11-12: [Temporary accounts](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:Temporary_accounts "Special:MyLanguage/Help:Temporary accounts") were deployed on Wikidata. From now on unregistered editors will get a temporary account automatically assigned to them, instead of being identified by their IP addresses.

From mediawiki.org

## MediaWiki is a collaboration and documentation platform brought to you by a vibrant community.

Photo of participants of the [Wikimedia Hackathon 2025](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Hackathon_2025 "Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Hackathon 2025")

The MediaWiki software is used by [tens of thousands of websites](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Sites_using_MediaWiki "Special:MyLanguage/Sites using MediaWiki") and [thousands of companies and organisations](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/MediaWiki_testimonials "Special:MyLanguage/MediaWiki testimonials").
It powers Wikipedia and also this website.
MediaWiki helps you collect and organise knowledge and make it available to people.
It's powerful, [multilingual](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Localisation "Special:MyLanguage/Localisation"), [free and open](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/FLOSS "w:FLOSS"), extensible, customisable, reliable, and free of charge.
[Find out more](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Manual:What_is_MediaWiki%3F "Special:MyLanguage/Manual:What is MediaWiki?") and [if MediaWiki is right for you](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Manual:Deciding_whether_to_use_a_wiki_as_your_website_type "Special:MyLanguage/Manual:Deciding whether to use a wiki as your website type").

### Set up and run MediaWiki

- [Download](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Download "Special:MyLanguage/Download"), [install](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Manual:Installing_MediaWiki "Special:MyLanguage/Manual:Installing MediaWiki") and [configure](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Manual:System_administration "Special:MyLanguage/Manual:System administration") MediaWiki
- Add functionality by installing [extensions](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Manual:Extensions "Special:MyLanguage/Manual:Extensions")
- Problems? See [errors and symptoms](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Manual:Common_errors_and_symptoms "Special:MyLanguage/Manual:Common errors and symptoms") and [FAQ](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Manual:FAQ "Special:MyLanguage/Manual:FAQ")
- Don't own a server? Find [hosting services](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Hosting_services "Special:MyLanguage/Hosting services")
- [Get professional development and consulting](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Professional_development_and_consulting "Special:MyLanguage/Professional development and consulting")
- Join [MediaWiki Stakeholders](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/MediaWiki_Stakeholders%27_Group "Special:MyLanguage/MediaWiki Stakeholders' Group") user group

### Edit and use MediaWiki

- [Learn how to navigate](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:Navigation "Special:MyLanguage/Help:Navigation")
- [Learn how to edit a page](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:Editing_pages "Special:MyLanguage/Help:Editing pages")
- [Learn more about reading, editing, and personal customisation](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:Contents "Special:MyLanguage/Help:Contents")

### Develop and extend code

- Read the MediaWiki [developer documentation](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Developer_hub "Special:MyLanguage/Developer hub")
- Visit the [Wikimedia Developer Portal](https://developer.wikimedia.org)

### Get help and contribute

- Cannot find the answer to a problem with MediaWiki? Ask the [support desk](/wiki/Project:Support_desk "Project:Support desk")!
- [Get involved](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/How_to_contribute "Special:MyLanguage/How to contribute") as a translator, designer, documentation writer, tester, tech ambassador, or developer
- [Report wrong software behaviour or a feature proposal](/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/How_to_report_a_bug "Special:MyLanguage/How to report a bug")
